***бидон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бидон.html>бидо́н</a> (15801)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bidon</i> in the late 19th century (attested since 1880), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">bidon</i>, further origin uncertain.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бидон.html>бидо́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bidón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бидон.html>бидо́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бидон.html>бидо́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бидон.html>бидо́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>can (large metallic or plastic cylindrical container with lid or cover, intended to hold liquids)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бидон.html>бидо́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молока́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bidón</b> dlja moloká</i> ― <span class="e-translation">milk can</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***билет.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> (1251)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">billet</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bilét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ticket (admission to entertainment or transportation)</li>
<li>banknote</li>
<li>membership card</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The noun <b><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a></b> in a sense of a ticket can be further described with <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>. For example on entertainment:
</p>
<dl><dd><ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опера.html>о́перу</a> (<i>opera ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цирк.html>цирк</a> (<i>circus ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:балет.html>бале́т</a> (<i>ballet ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>вечер</a> (<i>soiree ticket</i>)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:концерт.html>конце́рт</a> (<i>concert ticket</i>)</li>

***бирка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бирка.html>би́рка</a> (25625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unclear. There are several hypotheses: a borrowing from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:North Germanic languages">North Germanic</a></span> word for birch, compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">birk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">bjerk</i>; a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing, compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">bir + iki</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one + two</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; or a derivation from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">събьрати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭbĭrati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to assemble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собирать.html>собира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bьrati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бирка.html>би́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bírka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бирка.html>би́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бирка.html>би́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бирка.html>би́рок</a></b>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бирюза́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">birjuzá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бирюзовый.html>бирюзо́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">birjuzóvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> turquoise <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stone or color</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel">turquoise colour: <span style="background-color:48D1CC; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бирюзовый.html>бирюзо́вый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>birjuzóvyj</b> cvet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">turquoise <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">color</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>turquoise</b> color</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бирюзовый.html>бирюзо́вый</a></b> зиморо́док</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>birjuzóvyj</b> zimoródok</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/shining-blue_kingfisher" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:shining-blue kingfisher">shining-blue kingfisher</a></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>turquoise</b> kingfisher</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***бисер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бисер.html>би́сер</a> (20745)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">бисьръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bisĭrŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pearls</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgar language">Bulgar</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">بُسْر</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">busr</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unripe dates</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from the root <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">ب س ر</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">b-s-r</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> related to things being early, so applied to pearls because unripe dates can have some tactile and optical properties similar to pearls.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бисер.html>би́сер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bíser</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бисер.html>би́сера</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>beads
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышивать.html>вышива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бисер.html>би́сером</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vyšivátʹ bíserom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bead</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышивка.html>вы́шивка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бисер.html>би́сером</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výšivka bíserom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">beading, beadwork</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бисер.html>би́сер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свинья.html>сви́ньями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">metátʹ bíser péred svínʹjami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cast pearls before swine</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***бистро.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бистро.html>бистро́</a> (30090)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bistro</i>, according to folk etymology version borrowed from Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">býstro</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> "quickly" in 1814, when Russian Army was in Paris.
</p><p>In actual fact, the word is pure French, first attested only in 1884, possibly from <i>bistingot</i> (pub).
Especially the last letter 't' completely excludes Russian origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бистро.html>бистро́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bistró</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>bistro</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>би<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>стро́</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, несклоняемое (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 0  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_4">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:биток.html>бито́к</a> (12929)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:биток.html>бито́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bitók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>битка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:биток.html>битки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:биток.html>битко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cue ball</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">usually in the plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> round rissole, meatball</li></ol>

<p><b>би́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тый</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.  <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>  — <a href = vnd.unilang:побитый.html>поби́тый</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-би-</b>; суффикс: <b>-т</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***бить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a> (730)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*biti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*BʰeyH-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побить.html>поби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to beat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ше</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́тель</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бьёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ученик.html>ученика́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V náše vrémja učítelʹ nikogdá ne <b>bʹjót</b> učeniká.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">In our time the teacher never beats the student.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладоши.html>ладо́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bitʹ</b> v ladóši</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to clap (palms), causing applause</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:режиссер.html>Режиссёр</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:привычка.html>привы́чку</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладоши.html>ладо́ши</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:привлечь.html>привле́чь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ние</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Režissjór iméjet privýčku <b>bitʹ v ladóši</b> štóby privléčʹ vnimánije.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The producer has the habit of clapping to attract attention.</span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to chime <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a clock</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бью́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шне</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Časý <b>bʹjut</b> na bášne.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The clock chimes on the top of the tower.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to churn</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***биться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:биться.html>би́ться</a> (2526)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:биться.html>би́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поби́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fight, to struggle</li>
<li>to hit <i>(against)</i>, to knock <i>(against)</i>, to strike</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of heart</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to beat, to pulsate</li>
<li>to writhe, to toss about</li>
<li>to exercise oneself, to drudge, to toil</li>
<li>to break, to smash</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***битюг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:битюг.html>битю́г</a> (30142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Named after Bityug river near Voronezh, ultimately from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:битюг.html>битю́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bitjúg</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:битюг.html>битюга́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:битюг.html>битюги́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:битюг.html>битюго́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Beetewk <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a type of Russian heavy draft horse</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a very strong, heavily built man</li></ol>
